<div dir="auto" class="body markup"><p><span>I’ve solved over 2,000 coding problems across</span><strong> </strong><span>LeetCode</span><strong> </strong><span>and other platforms</span><strong>, </strong><span>and</span><strong> </strong><span>if there’s one thing I’ve learned, it’s this:</span></p><blockquote><p><span>Getting good at DSA is </span><strong>less</strong><span> about how many problems you solve and </span><strong>more</strong><span> about how many </span><strong>patterns</strong><span> you truly understand.</span></p></blockquote><p>Patterns help you solve a wide range of problems in less time because they train you to recognize the right approach, even for questions you have never seen before.</p><p><span>In this article, I’ll walk you through the </span><strong>20 most important patterns</strong><span> that made learning DSA and preparing for coding interviews far less painful for me.</span></p><p><span>Even better, these are the same patterns that showed up again and again in my interviews, including at companies like </span><strong>Amazon</strong><span> and </span><strong>Google</strong><span>.</span></p><div class="captioned-image-container"><figure><a walkthrough</p></li><li><p>Practice links to related LeetCode problems</p></li></ul><p>This article is the essence of everything I have learned about DSA and LeetCode, distilled into one guide. I’ve also added links for each pattern so you can dive deeper when you’re ready.</p><p><span>If you want to explore more patterns and resources, check out: </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/" rel="">algomaster.io</a></p><p>Let’s get started.</p><p Sum</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§1-prefix-sum" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/1-prefix-sum" 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h1><div class="captioned-image-container"><figure><a target="_blank" data-attrs="{&quot;src&quot;:&quot;https://substack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com/public/images/34681b04-c8c1-489e-bb28-5a7bac0e8748_395x212.png&quot;,&quot;srcNoWatermark&quot;:null,&quot;fullscreen&quot;:null,&quot;imageSize&quot;:null,&quot;height&quot;:212,&quot;width&quot;:395,&quot;resizeWidth&quot;:null,&quot;bytes&quot;:13267,&quot;alt&quot;:null,&quot;title&quot;:null,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;image/png&quot;,&quot;href&quot;:null,&quot;belowTheFold&quot;:true,&quot;topImage&quot;:false,&quot;internalRedirect&quot;:&quot;https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210?img=https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F34681b04-c8c1-489e-bb28-5a7bac0e8748_395x212.png&quot;,&quot;isProcessing&quot;:false,&quot;align&quot;:null,&quot;offset&quot;:false}" 424w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!mhMA!,w_848,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F34681b04-c8c1-489e-bb28-5a7bac0e8748_395x212.png 848w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!mhMA!,w_1272,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F34681b04-c8c1-489e-bb28-5a7bac0e8748_395x212.png 1272w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!mhMA!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F34681b04-c8c1-489e-bb28-5a7bac0e8748_395x212.png 1456w" sizes="100vw" loading="lazy" class="sizing-normal"></picture><div></div></div></a></figure></div><p><span>The Prefix Sum pattern involves </span><strong>preprocessing</strong><span> an array to create a new array where each element at index </span><code>i</code><span> represents the sum of all elements from the start up to </span><code>i</code><span>. This allows for </span><strong>O(1) sum queries</strong><span> on any subarray.</span></p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="ininik"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Multiple sum queries on subarrays</p></li><li><p>Finding subarrays with a target sum</p></li><li><p>Calculating cumulative totals</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="usfdah"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>// Build prefix sum array
int[] prefix = new int[n + 1];
for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {
    prefix[i + 1] = prefix[i] + nums[i];
}

// Query sum of range [left, right]
int rangeSum = prefix[right + 1] - prefix[left];</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="36q5c9"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Range Sum Query</strong><span>: Given an array </span><code>nums</code><span>, answer multiple queries about the sum of elements within a specific range </span><code>[i, j]</code><span>.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="jz25aq"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>nums = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6]</code><span>, </span><code>i = 1</code><span>, </span><code>j = 3</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>9</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="crnq7"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>nums = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6]

Step 1: Build prefix sum array
  prefix[0] = 0
  prefix[1] = 0 + 1 = 1
  prefix[2] = 1 + 2 = 3
  prefix[3] = 3 + 3 = 6
  prefix[4] = 6 + 4 = 10
  prefix[5] = 10 + 5 = 15
  prefix[6] = 15 + 6 = 21

  prefix = [0, 1, 3, 6, 10, 15, 21]

Step 2: Query sum for range [1, 3]
  sum = prefix[3 + 1] - prefix[1]
  sum = prefix[4] - prefix[1]
  sum = 10 - 1 = 9</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="l4wzo"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 rel="">Product of Array Except Self (LeetCode #238)</a></p></li></ol><div><hr></div><h1 class="header-anchor-post"><span>2. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/two-pointers-introduction" rel="">Two Pointers</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset 848w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!c0Qf!,w_1272,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fe2bc6864-ae2a-4634-bfea-c270a62a05c3_427x213.png 1272w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!c0Qf!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2Fe2bc6864-ae2a-4634-bfea-c270a62a05c3_427x213.png 1456w" sizes="100vw" loading="lazy" class="sizing-normal"></picture><div></div></div></a></figure></div><p><span>The Two Pointers pattern uses two pointers to traverse an array or list, typically from opposite ends or both moving in the same direction. It reduces time complexity from </span><strong>O(n^2) to O(n)</strong><span> for many problems.</span></p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="rfqypy"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Finding pairs in sorted arrays</p></li><li><p>Comparing elements from both ends</p></li><li><p>Partitioning arrays</p></li><li><p>Palindrome checks</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="136vml"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>// Opposite direction (converging)
int left = 0, right = n - 1;
while (left &lt; right) {
    if (condition_met) {
        // found answer
    } else if (need_larger_sum) {
        left++;
    } else {
        right--;
    }
}

// Same direction
int slow = 0;
for (int fast = 0; fast &lt; n; fast++) {
    if (condition) {
        // process and move slow
        slow++;
    }
}</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="fmttcm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Two Sum II</strong><span>: Find two numbers in a sorted array that add up to a target value. Return their indices.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="2634d"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>nums = [1, 2, 3, 4, 6]</code><span>, </span><code>target = 6</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>[1, 3]</code><span> (indices of 2 and 4)</span></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="smg2ge"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>nums = [1, 2, 3, 4, 6], target = 6

Step 1: left = 0, right = 4
  sum = nums[0] + nums[4] = 1 + 6 = 7 &gt; 6
  Move right pointer left: right = 3

Step 2: left = 0, right = 3
  sum = nums[0] + nums[3] = 1 + 4 = 5 &lt; 6
  Move left pointer right: left = 1

Step 3: left = 1, right = 3
  sum = nums[1] + nums[3] = 2 + 4 = 6 == target
  Found! Return [1, 3]</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/two-sum-ii-input-array-is-sorted/" rel="">Two Sum II - Input Array is Sorted (LeetCode 9"></polyline><polyline points="9 21 3 21 3 15"></polyline><line x1="21" x2="14" y1="3" y2="10"></line><line x1="3" x2="10" y1="21" y2="14"></line></svg></button></div></div></div></a></figure></div><p>The Sliding Window pattern maintains a window of elements and slides it across the array to find subarrays or substrings that satisfy certain conditions. It avoids recalculating overlapping parts of consecutive windows.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="6fo3yh"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Contiguous subarray/substring problems</p></li><li><p>Finding maximum/minimum in window of size k</p></li><li><p>Longest/shortest substring with certain properties</p></li><li><p>Problems involving consecutive elements</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="flsck"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>// Fixed-size window
int windowSum = 0;
for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {
    windowSum += nums[i];
    if (i &gt;= k - 1) {
        // process window
        result = Math.max(result, windowSum);
        windowSum -= nums[i - k + 1];
    }
}

// Variable-size window
int left = 0;
for (int right = 0; right &lt; n; right++) {
    // expand window by including nums[right]

    while (window_condition_violated) {
        // shrink window from left
        left++;
    }

    // update result
}</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="35zh6q"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Maximum Sum Subarray of Size K</strong><span>: Find the maximum sum of any contiguous subarray of size </span><code>k</code><span>.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="se22v"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>nums = [2, 1, 5, 1, 3, 2]</code><span>, </span><code>k = 3</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>9</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="ummxv"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>nums = [2, 1, 5, 1, 3, 2], k = 3

Step 1: Build initial window [2, 1, 5]
  windowSum = 2 + 1 + 5 = 8
  maxSum = 8

Step 2: Slide window to [1, 5, 1]
  windowSum = 8 - 2 + 1 = 7
  maxSum = max(8, 7) = 8

Step 3: Slide window to [5, 1, 3]
  windowSum = 7 - 1 + 3 = 9
  maxSum = max(8, 9) = 9

Step 4: Slide window to [1, 3, 2]
  windowSum = 9 - 5 + 2 = 6
  maxSum = max(9, 6) = 9

Result: 9</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/maximum-average-subarray-i/" rel="">Maximum Average Subarray I (LeetCode rel="">Sliding Window Maximum (LeetCode #239)</a></p></li></ol><div><hr></div><h1 class="header-anchor-post"><span>4. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/fast-slow-pointers-introduction" https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!dGnL!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F35244893-2102-4209-a164-1709d042b95f_553x164.png 1456w" sizes="100vw" loading="lazy" class="sizing-normal"></picture><div></div></div></a></figure></div><p>The Fast &amp; Slow Pointers pattern (also called Tortoise and Hare) uses two pointers moving at different speeds. When there is a cycle, the fast pointer will eventually meet the slow pointer.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="w30ye"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Detecting cycles in linked lists or arrays</p></li><li><p>Finding the middle of a linked list</p></li><li><p>Finding the start of a cycle</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="4h99vn"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code><code>// Find middle
while (fast != null &amp;&amp; fast.next != null) {
    slow = slow.next;
    fast = fast.next.next;
}
return slow; // middle node

// Cycle detection
ListNode slow = head, fast = head;
while (fast != null &amp;&amp; fast.next != null) {
    slow = slow.next;
    fast = fast.next.next;

    if (slow == fast) {
        // cycle detected
        return true;
    }
}
return false; // no cycle</code></code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="g8aftt"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Linked List Cycle</strong><span>: Detect if a linked list has a cycle.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="jwonnp"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>head = [3, 2, 0, -4]</code><span>, tail connects to node index 1</span></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>true</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="t93v4"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code><code>List: 3 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 0 -&gt; -4 -&gt; (back to 2)

Step 1: slow = 3, fast = 3
Step 2: slow = 2, fast = 0
Step 3: slow = 0, fast = 2 (wrapped around)
Step 4: slow = -4, fast = -4

slow == fast, cycle detected!</code></code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="hsspqi"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" class="header-anchor-post"><span>5. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/linked-list-in-place-reversal-introduction" rel="">LinkedList In-place Reversal</a><div class="pencraft 1456w" sizes="100vw" loading="lazy" class="sizing-normal"></picture><div></div></div></a></figure></div><p>This pattern reverses parts of a linked list without using extra space. It manipulates pointers to reverse the direction of links.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="ohq3id"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Reversing a linked list or portion of it</p></li><li><p>Reversing nodes in groups</p></li><li><p>Checking for palindromes in linked lists</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="mfcgpa"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>// Reverse entire list
ListNode prev = null, curr = head;
while (curr != null) {
    ListNode next = curr.next;
    curr.next = prev;
    prev = curr;
    curr = next;
}
return prev; // new head</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="eezeee"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Reverse Linked List II</strong><span>: Reverse the nodes of a linked list from position </span><code>m</code><span> to </span><code>n</code><span>.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="jlxp2o"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>head = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]</code><span>, </span><code>m = 2</code><span>, </span><code>n = 4</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>[1, 4, 3, 2, 5]</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="01naba"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>Original: 1 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 3 -&gt; 4 -&gt; 5
Reverse positions 2 to 4

Step 1: Position prev before node 2
  prev = 1, curr = 2

Step 2: Move 3 after 1
  1 -&gt; 3 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 4 -&gt; 5

Step 3: Move 4 after 1
  1 -&gt; 4 -&gt; 3 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 5

Result: [1, 4, 3, 2, 5]</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-linked-list/" rel="">Reverse Linked List (LeetCode #206)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-linked-list-ii/" rel="">Reverse Linked List II (LeetCode #92)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/swap-nodes-in-pairs/" rel="">Swap Nodes in Pairs (LeetCode #24)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-nodes-in-k-group/" rel="">Reverse Nodes in k-Group (LeetCode #25)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/palindrome-linked-list/" rel="">Palindrome Linked List (LeetCode #234)</a></p></li></ol><div><hr></div><h1 class="header-anchor-post"><span>6. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/frequency-counting-introduction" rel="">Frequency Counting</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§6-frequency-counting" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/6-frequency-counting" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="hg7bfm"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h1><p>The Frequency Counting pattern uses hash maps or arrays to count occurrences of elements. It transforms O(n^2) lookup problems into O(n) by trading space for time.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="t5gtpr"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Finding duplicates or unique elements</p></li><li><p>Checking if two collections have same elements</p></li><li><p>Finding elements that appear k times</p></li><li><p>Anagram problems</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="66wkfg"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code><code>// Using HashMap
Map&lt;Integer, Integer&gt; freq = new HashMap&lt;&gt;();
for (int num : nums) {
    freq.put(num, freq.getOrDefault(num, 0) + 1);
}

// Using array (when range is known)
int[] freq = new int[26]; // for lowercase letters
for (char c : str.toCharArray()) {
    freq[c - 'a']++;
}

// Finding element with specific frequency
for (Map.Entry&lt;Integer, Integer&gt; entry : freq.entrySet()) {
    if (entry.getValue() == target) {
        return entry.getKey();
    }
}</code></code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="pjrpq"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Valid Anagram</strong><span>: Given two strings </span><code>s</code><span> and </span><code>t</code><span>, return true if </span><code>t</code><span> is an anagram of </span><code>s</code><span>.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="w4qco"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>s = "anagram"</code><span>, </span><code>t = "nagaram"</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>true</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="yb2e4"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code><code>s = "anagram", t = "nagaram"

Step 1: Count frequencies in s
  freq = {a: 3, n: 1, g: 1, r: 1, m: 1}

Step 2: Decrement frequencies using t
  't' -&gt; n: freq[n] = 1 - 1 = 0
  't' -&gt; a: freq[a] = 3 - 1 = 2
  't' -&gt; g: freq[g] = 1 - 1 = 0
  't' -&gt; a: freq[a] = 2 - 1 = 1
  't' -&gt; r: freq[r] = 1 - 1 = 0
  't' -&gt; a: freq[a] = 1 - 1 = 0
  't' -&gt; m: freq[m] = 1 - 1 = 0

Step 3: Check all frequencies are 0
  freq = {a: 0, n: 0, g: 0, r: 0, m: 0}
  All zero -&gt; Return true</code></code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/valid-anagram/" rel="">Valid Anagram (LeetCode #242)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/group-anagrams/" rel="">Group Anagrams (LeetCode #49)</a></p></li><li><p><a class="header-anchor-post"><span>7. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/monotonic-stack-introduction" rel="">Monotonic Stack</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§7-monotonic-stack" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor 1456w" sizes="100vw" loading="lazy" class="sizing-normal"></picture><div></div></div></a></figure></div><p>A Monotonic Stack maintains elements in either increasing or decreasing order. As you iterate, you pop elements that violate the order, which reveals relationships between elements.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="vw719h"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Finding the next greater/smaller element</p></li><li><p>Finding previous greater/smaller element</p></li><li><p>Problems involving spans or ranges</p></li><li><p>Histogram problems</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="9bsblb"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>/// Next Greater Element (decreasing stack)
int[] result = new int[n];
Arrays.fill(result, -1);
Stack&lt;Integer&gt; stack = new Stack&lt;&gt;(); // stores indices

for (int i = 0; i &lt; n; i++) {
    while (!stack.isEmpty() &amp;&amp; nums[i] &gt; nums[stack.peek()]) {
        int idx = stack.pop();
        result[idx] = nums[i];
    }
    stack.push(i);
}</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="yce34"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Next Greater Element</strong><span>: For each element in an array, find the next greater element. Output -1 if none exists.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="an4m6"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>nums = [2, 1, 2, 4, 3]</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>[4, 2, 4, -1, -1]</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="9296mb"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>nums = [2, 1, 2, 4, 3]
result = [-1, -1, -1, -1, -1]
stack = []

Step 1: i = 0, nums[0] = 2
  stack is empty, push 0
  stack = [0]

Step 2: i = 1, nums[1] = 1
  1 &lt; nums[0]=2, push 1
  stack = [0, 1]

Step 3: i = 2, nums[2] = 2
  2 &gt; nums[1]=1, pop 1, result[1] = 2
  2 &lt;= nums[0]=2, push 2
  stack = [0, 2], result = [-1, 2, -1, -1, -1]

Step 4: i = 3, nums[3] = 4
  4 &gt; nums[2]=2, pop 2, result[2] = 4
  4 &gt; nums[0]=2, pop 0, result[0] = 4
  push 3
  stack = [3], result = [4, 2, 4, -1, -1]

Step 5: i = 4, nums[4] = 3
  3 &lt; nums[3]=4, push 4
  stack = [3, 4]

Result: [4, 2, 4, -1, -1]</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="nglfi"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/next-greater-element-i/" rel="">Next Greater Element I (LeetCode #496)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/daily-temperatures/" rel="">Daily Temperatures (LeetCode #739)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/trapping-rain-water/" rel="">Trapping Rain Water (LeetCode #42)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/online-stock-span/" rel="">Online Stock Span (LeetCode #901)</a></p></li></ol><div><hr></div><h1 class="header-anchor-post"><span>8. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/bit-manipulation-introduction" rel="">Bit Manipulation</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§8-bit-manipulation" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/8-bit-manipulation" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="tviqed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h1><p>Bit manipulation uses binary operations (AND, OR, XOR, NOT, shifts) to solve problems efficiently. XOR is particularly useful since a ^ a = 0 and a ^ 0 = a.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="net6r"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Finding unique numbers (XOR)</p></li><li><p>Checking power of 2</p></li><li><p>Counting bits</p></li><li><p>Generating subsets using bit masks</p></li><li><p>Space optimization</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="7h51oq"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>// Basic operations
int and = a &amp; b;        // both bits 1
int or = a | b;         // either bit 1
int xor = a ^ b;        // bits different
int not = ~a;           // flip bits
int leftShift = a &lt;&lt; n; // multiply by 2^n
int rightShift = a &gt;&gt; n;// divide by 2^n

// Check if bit i is set
boolean isSet = (n &amp; (1 &lt;&lt; i)) != 0;

// Set bit i
n = n | (1 &lt;&lt; i);

// Clear bit i
n = n &amp; ~(1 &lt;&lt; i);

// Toggle bit i
n = n ^ (1 &lt;&lt; i);

// Check if power of 2
boolean isPowerOf2 = (n &gt; 0) &amp;&amp; ((n &amp; (n - 1)) == 0);

// Count set bits
int count = 0;
while (n &gt; 0) {
    count += n &amp; 1;
    n &gt;&gt;= 1;
}
// Or: Integer.bitCount(n);

// Find single number (XOR all elements)
int single = 0;
for (int num : nums) {
    single ^= num;
}</code></pre><h2 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="4sjzz"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h2><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/" rel="">Single Number (LeetCode #136)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/" rel="">Number of 1 Bits (LeetCode #191)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/" rel="">Counting Bits (LeetCode #338)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/power-of-two/" rel="">Power of Two (LeetCode #231)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/missing-number/" rel="">Missing Number (LeetCode #268)</a></p></li></ol><div><hr></div><h1 class="header-anchor-post"><span>9. </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/top-k-elements-introduction" rel="">Top ‘K’ Elements</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§9-top-k-elements" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/9-top-k-elements" https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!yX7t!,w_848,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F2546e104-3d19-49ec-b7bb-1652786a4a79_597x240.png 848w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!yX7t!,w_1272,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F2546e104-3d19-49ec-b7bb-1652786a4a79_597x240.png 1272w, https://substackcdn.com/image/fetch/$s_!yX7t!,w_1456,c_limit,f_auto,q_auto:good,fl_progressive:steep/https%3A%2F%2Fsubstack-post-media.s3.amazonaws.com%2Fpublic%2Fimages%2F2546e104-3d19-49ec-b7bb-1652786a4a79_597x240.png 1456w" sizes="100vw" loading="lazy" class="sizing-normal"></picture><div></div></div></a></figure></div><p>This pattern finds the k largest or smallest elements using heaps (priority queues). A min-heap of size k keeps track of k largest elements, and a max-heap keeps k smallest.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="u27ozb"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Finding k largest/smallest elements</p></li><li><p>Finding kth largest/smallest element</p></li><li><p>Finding k most/least frequent elements</p></li><li><p>Merging k sorted lists</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Template<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§template" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/template" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="qv8rnh"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><pre><code>// K largest elements using min-heap
PriorityQueue&lt;Integer&gt; minHeap = new PriorityQueue&lt;&gt;();

for (int num : nums) {
    minHeap.offer(num);
    if (minHeap.size() &gt; k) {
        minHeap.poll(); // remove smallest
    }
}
// minHeap now contains k largest elements
// minHeap.peek() is the kth largest</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="ulfiik"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Kth Largest Element</strong><span>: Find the kth largest element in an unsorted array.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="6rnbtu"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> </span><code>nums = [3, 2, 1, 5, 6, 4]</code><span>, </span><code>k = 2</code></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> </span><code>5</code></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="pojt37"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>nums = [3, 2, 1, 5, 6, 4], k = 2
Using min-heap of size k

Step 1: num = 3
  heap = [3]

Step 2: num = 2
  heap = [2, 3]

Step 3: num = 1
  heap = [1, 3, 2], size &gt; k
  poll smallest: heap = [2, 3]

Step 4: num = 5
  heap = [2, 3, 5], size &gt; k
  poll smallest: heap = [3, 5]

Step 5: num = 6
  heap = [3, 5, 6], size &gt; k
  poll smallest: heap = [5, 6]

Step 6: num = 4
  heap = [4, 6, 5], size &gt; k
  poll smallest: heap = [5, 6]

heap.peek() = 5 (kth largest)</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/kth-largest-element-in-an-array/" rel="">Kth Largest Element in an Array (LeetCode #215)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/top-k-frequent-elements/" rel="">Top K Frequent Elements (LeetCode #347)</a></p></li><li><p><a </span><a href="https://algomaster.io/learn/dsa/intervals-introduction" rel="">Overlapping Intervals</a><div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset
