9"></polyline><polyline points="9 21 3 21 3 15"></polyline><line x1="21" x2="14" y1="3" y2="10"></line><line x1="3" x2="10" y1="21" y2="14"></line></svg></button></div></div></div></a></figure></div><p>Dynamic Programming (DP) solves problems by breaking them into overlapping subproblems and storing results to avoid recomputation. It works when problems have optimal substructure.</p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">When to use<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/when-to-use" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="wab02a"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ul><li><p>Problems with overlapping subproblems</p></li><li><p>Optimization (min/max) problems</p></li><li><p>Counting problems (number of ways)</p></li><li><p>Decision problems (can we achieve X?)</p></li></ul><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Common DP Patterns<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§common-dp-patterns" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/common-dp-patterns" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="qcea4m"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><strong>Fibonacci Pattern</strong><span> (1D DP with previous states)</span></p></li><li><p><strong>0/1 Knapsack</strong><span> (include or exclude each item)</span></p></li><li><p><strong>Longest Common Subsequence</strong><span> (2D DP on two sequences)</span></p></li><li><p><strong>Longest Increasing Subsequence</strong></p></li></ol><p><span>You can find more DP patterns and how to approach them in </span><a href="https://blog.algomaster.io/p/20-patterns-to-master-dynamic-programming" rel="">this article</a><span>.</span></p><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Sample Problem<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/sample-problem" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="gdpsx"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><p><strong>Climbing Stairs</strong><span>: Find the number of ways to climb n stairs, taking 1 or 2 steps at a time.</span></p><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Example:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§example" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/example" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="ozhiut"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><ul><li><p><strong>Input:</strong><span> n = 4</span></p></li><li><p><strong>Output:</strong><span> 5</span></p></li></ul><h4 class="header-anchor-post">Step-by-Step Walkthrough:<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/step-by-step-walkthrough" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="c75wgr"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h4><pre><code>n = 4

dp[i] = number of ways to reach step i
dp[i] = dp[i-1] + dp[i-2]
(we can reach step i from step i-1 or step i-2)

Base cases:
  dp[0] = 1 (one way to stay at ground)
  dp[1] = 1 (one way: take 1 step)

Step 2: dp[2] = dp[1] + dp[0] = 1 + 1 = 2
  Ways: [1,1], [2]

Step 3: dp[3] = dp[2] + dp[1] = 2 + 1 = 3
  Ways: [1,1,1], [1,2], [2,1]

Step 4: dp[4] = dp[3] + dp[2] = 3 + 2 = 5
  Ways: [1,1,1,1], [1,1,2], [1,2,1], [2,1,1], [2,2]

Result: 5 ways</code></pre><h3 class="header-anchor-post">Practice Problems<div class="pencraft pc-display-flex pc-alignItems-center pc-position-absolute pc-reset header-anchor-parent"><div class="pencraft pc-display-contents pc-reset pubTheme-yiXxQA"><div id="§practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset header-anchor offset-top"></div><button tabindex="0" type="button" aria-label="Link" data-href="https://blog.algomaster.io/i/184854210/practice-problems" class="pencraft pc-reset pencraft iconButton-mq_Et5 iconButtonBase-dJGHgN buttonBase-GK1x3M buttonStyle-r7yGCK size_sm-G3LciD priority_secondary-S63h9o" fdprocessedid="5cwse"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></button></div></div></h3><ol><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/climbing-stairs/" rel="">Climbing Stairs (LeetCode #70)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/house-robber/" rel="">House Robber (LeetCode #198)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change/" rel="">Coin Change (LeetCode #322)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-common-subsequence/" rel="">Longest Common Subsequence (LeetCode #1143)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-increasing-subsequence/" rel="">Longest Increasing Subsequence (LeetCode #300)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-equal-subset-sum/" rel="">Partition Equal Subset Sum (LeetCode #416)</a></p></li><li><p><a href="https://leetcode.com/problems/edit-distance/" rel="">Edit Distance (LeetCode #72)</a></p></li></ol><div><hr></div><p>That’s it.
